[13/08/24, 5:33:55‚ÄØPM] Anthony-Agent-Friendly Realtors: BRH Agent: There are many Benefits for MSME Registration in India.

The key area for us is, has been & will be is: 
*Protection against Delayed Payments:*
The purchasers of goods or services from SSIs or MSMEs occasionally tend to put off making payments. By granting them the ability to charge interest on delayed payments from the buyer's side, the Ministry of Micro, Small and Medium Enterprise supports these businesses. Such conflicts must be arbitrated and mediated within a reasonable time.

The buyer is required to make the payment within 15 days of the day they accepted the products and services from or on or before the payment date that an MSME or SCI-registered firm mutually agreed upon if any MSME-registered enterprise provides goods or services to the buyer. It is only possible if there is no mention of the date of payment.

The buyer must pay compound interest in addition to interest (charged monthly) on the agreed-upon sum if the payment is delayed for more than 45 days after accepting the goods or services. The rate of interest is thrice what the Reserve Bank of India stated

In our Realtor world:
Buyer is referred to as Builder
